hast scourged seditious person terrible execution iustly inflicted disobedience thee thy seruaunt soueraine example v warnyng correction amendement thy seruauntes thyne accustomed goodnesse turnyng alwayes wickednesse euyll men profite feare thee thy iudgementes remembryng thy mercye hast thy assistaunce geuen victorye thy seruaunte queene true nobilitie faythfull subiectes litle rather effusion
